<P style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin:0;color:#000000'><B>Item 8.01.  Other Information.</B></P>

<P align=justify style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin:0;text-indent:36pt;color:#000000;background-color:#FFFFFF'>On December 6, 2021, the Company issued a press release announcing it has completed the FINRA corporate actions and steps required to effect the reverse stock split of its common stock at a ratio of 1-for-14. The Company also received approval to change its name to Idaho Strategic Resources, Inc. The Company&#8217;s stock will began trading on a post-split basis and under the new name of Idaho Strategic Resources, Inc. at the open of trading on December 6, 2021. Idaho Strategic Resources will continue to trade on the OTCQB under the symbol NJMCD for a period of 20 days following the Effective Date. Following the 20-day period the symbol will automatically revert to NJMC.</P>

<BODY>
<DIV style=margin-left:72pt;width:468pt><P style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>Exhibit 99.1</P>
<P style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:16pt Times New Roman;margin:0'><IMG src=nrex99z1_1.jpg width=172 height=79 alt='Picture 2' title='Picture 2'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=center style='font:16pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=center style='font:16pt Times New Roman;margin:0'><B>New Jersey Mining Completes Reverse Stock Split and Name Change to Idaho Strategic Resources, Inc.</B></P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>COEUR D'ALENE, Idaho, December 6, 2021 (ACCESSWIRE) -- New Jersey Mining Company (OTCQB: NJMCD)<FONT style='font:10pt Verdana'> </FONT>(&#8220;NJMC&#8221; or the &#8220;Company&#8221;) is pleased to announce it has completed the FINRA corporate actions and steps required to effect the reverse stock split of its common stock at a ratio of 1-for-14, as previously approved by shareholders. The Company also received approval to change its name to Idaho Strategic Resources, Inc., also approved by shareholders. The Company&#8217;s stock will begin trading on a post-split basis and under the new name of Idaho Strategic Resources, Inc. at the open of trading on December 6, 2021. Idaho Strategic Resources will continue to trade on the OTCQB under the symbol NJMCD for a period of 20 days following the Effective Date. Following the 20-day period the symbol will automatically revert to NJMC.</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>NJMC CEO and President John Swallow stated, &#8220;We continue advancing on a number of fronts &#8211;&nbsp;corporate, operations, personnel, exploration, etc. The FINRA approval was required to change our name and continue with up-listing to the NYSE American, and the next steps are underway. In addition to gold and real estate as historically recognized stores of value, we feel our domestic rare earth element (and associated energy) positioning provides stakeholders with a desirable early-stage risk/reward scenario. The anticipated supply/demand profiles in these nascent yet vital industries are adding to what is already a very exciting time for our company.&#8221; </P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>At the effective time of the reverse stock split, every fourteen (14) shares of New Jersey Mining Company&#8217;s issued and outstanding common stock will be automatically converted into one (1) issued and outstanding share of Idaho Strategic Resources, Inc. common stock, without any change in the par value per share. </P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0;background-color:#FFFFFF'>Shareholders holding shares through a brokerage account will have their shares automatically adjusted to reflect the reverse stock split and name change. No fractional interest in a share of common stock will be deliverable upon the effectiveness of the reverse stock split. All shares of common stock (including fractions thereof) held by a holder immediately prior to the reverse stock split will be aggregated for purposes of determining whether the reverse stock split would result in a fractional share. Any fractional share resulting from such aggregation of common stock as of the reverse stock split will be rounded up and converted to the nearest whole share of common stock. The reverse stock split will reduce the number of shares of Idaho Strategic Resources common stock outstanding from approximately 150.6 million shares, based on the Company&#8217;s shares outstanding as of December 6, 2021, to approximately 10.7 million shares. </P>
<HR style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'><P align=center style='font:11pt Calibri;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><FONT style='font-family:Times New Roman'>Idaho Strategic Resources, Inc. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT style='font:12pt Times New Roman'>&#8226;</FONT><FONT style='font-family:Times New Roman'> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;201 N. 3<SUP>rd</SUP> Street &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</FONT><FONT style='font:12pt Times New Roman'>&#8226;</FONT><FONT style='font-family:Times New Roman'> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Coeur d&#8217;Alene, Idaho 83814</FONT></P>
<P align=center style='font:11pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>1</P>
<HR style='page-break-after:always;border:0;height:3pt;background-color:#909090;margin:8pt 0'><P style=line-height:0;margin:0></P>
<P style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'><FONT style='border-bottom:1px solid #000000'><B>About </B><B>Idaho Strategic Resources</B><B>, Inc.</B></FONT></P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:6pt'>Headquartered in North Idaho, Idaho Strategic Resources, Inc. is the rare example of a vertically integrated, operating junior mining company. Idaho Strategic Resources produces gold at the Golden Chest Mine and has consolidated the Murray Gold Belt (MGB) for the first time in over 100-years. The MGB is an overlooked gold producing region within the Coeur d&#8217;Alene Mining District, located north of the prolific Silver Valley. In addition to gold and gold production, the Company maintains a strategic and domestic presence in the Critical Minerals sector and is focused on advancing its officially recognized Diamond Creek and Roberts Rare Earth Element projects in central Idaho. Idaho Strategic Resources is one of the few companies possessing the combination of officially recognized U.S. based domestic rare earth element properties (in Idaho) and Idaho-based gold production in an established mining community.&#160;</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:6pt'>Idaho Strategic Resources possesses the in-house skillsets of a much larger company, from early-stage exploration and core drilling to mine development and production, including the design and operation of the New Jersey mill &#8211;&nbsp;all while enjoying the flexibility of a smaller and more entrepreneurial corporate structure. Its production-based strategy, by design, provides the flexibility to advance the Murray Gold Belt and/or its Critical Minerals holdings on its own or possibly with a strategic partner in a manner that is consistent with its existing philosophy and culture.</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:6pt'>Idaho Strategic Resources has established a high-quality, early to advanced-stage asset base in four historic mining districts of Idaho and Montana, which includes the currently producing Golden Chest Mine. Management is stakeholder focused and owns approximately 15-percent of NJMC common stock.</P>
<P align=justify style='font:12pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:10pt'>For more information on Idaho Strategic Resources   go to <FONT style='color:#0000FF;border-bottom:1px solid #0000FF'>www.newjerseymining.com</FONT> or call: </P>
